&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 1 -&amp;#160;&lt;i&gt;The Company and Summary of Significant Accounting&#13;Policies:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Bridgford Foods Corporation&#13;was organized in 1952. We originally began operations in 1932 as a retail meat market in San Diego, California and evolved into&#13;a meat wholesaler for hotels and restaurants, a distributor of frozen food products, a processor and packer of meat, and a manufacturer&#13;and distributor of frozen food products for sale on a retail and wholesale basis. We and our subsidiaries are primarily engaged&#13;in the manufacturing, marketing and distribution of an extensive line of frozen, refrigerated, and snack food products throughout&#13;the United States.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The consolidated financial&#13;statements include the accounts of the Company and its subsidiaries, all of which are wholly-owned. All inter-company transactions&#13;have been eliminated.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of estimates and assumptions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The preparation of financial&#13;statements in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make certain estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities at the date of the&#13;financial statements, as well as the reported revenues and expenses during the respective reporting periods. Actual results could&#13;differ from those estimates. Amounts estimated related to liabilities for pension benefits, self-insured workers&amp;#8217; compensation&#13;and employee healthcare benefits are subject to inherent uncertainties and these estimated liabilities may ultimately settle at&#13;amounts which may vary from current estimates. Other areas with underlying estimates include realization of deferred tax assets,&#13;cash surrender or contract value of life insurance policies, promotional allowances and the allowance for doubtful accounts and&#13;inventory reserves. Management believes its current estimates are reasonable and based on the best information available at the&#13;time.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We test long-lived assets&#13;for recoverability whenever events or changes in circumstances indicate that the carrying amount may not be recoverable. If an&#13;impairment is indicated, we measure the fair value of assets to determine if and when adjustments are recorded.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Subsequent events&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Management has evaluated&#13;events subsequent to November 1, 2019 through the date the accompanying consolidated financial statements were filed with the Securities&#13;and Exchange Commission for transactions and other events that may require adjustment of and/or disclosure in such financial statements.&#13;On December 19, 2019, we entered into a third master collateral loan and security agreement with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A for $3,750&#13;in equipment financing. Pursuant to the loan agreement, we borrowed $3,750 to purchase specific equipment for our new Chicago processing&#13;facility at a fixed rate of 3.70% per annum. The loan term is seven years and is secured by the purchased equipment. The funds&#13;were received on December 23, 2019. The master collateral loan and security agreement with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. contains various&#13;affirmative and negative covenants that limit the use of funds and define other provisions of the loan. The main financial covenants&#13;are listed below:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 11pt Calibri
 Helvetica
 Sans-Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Total Liabilities divided by Tangible Net Worth not greater than 2.5 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter,&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Quick Ratio not less than 1.0 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter end,&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Net income after taxes not less than one dollar on a quarterly basis, determined as of each fiscal quarter end.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The Company maintains a&#13;line of credit with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. that expires on March 1, 2020. Under the terms of this line of credit, we may borrow&#13;up to $7,500 at an interest rate equal to the bank&amp;#8217;s prime rate or LIBOR plus 1.5%. The Company borrowed $2,000 under this&#13;line of credit on November 24, 2019. The Company borrowed an additional 2.500,000 under the line of credit on January 24, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Based on management&amp;#8217;s&#13;review, no other material events were identified that require adjustment to the financial statements or additional disclosure.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Accounts Receivable&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Accounts receivable are&#13;recorded at net realizable value.&amp;#160; The value is presented net of allowance for doubtful accounts and promotional incentives.&amp;#160;&#13;Our accounts receivable consists mainly of trade receivables from customer sales.&amp;#160; We evaluate the collectability of our accounts&#13;receivable based on a several factors.&amp;#160; The provision for doubtful accounts receivable is based on historical trends and current&#13;collectability risk.&amp;#160; Our provision for doubtful accounts was $31 and $33 as of November 1, 2019 and November 2, 2018, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations of credit risk&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our credit risk is diversified&#13;across a broad range of customers and geographic regions. Losses due to credit risk have recently been immaterial. The carrying&#13;amount of cash equivalents, accounts and other receivables, accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximate fair market value&#13;due to the short maturity of these instruments. We maintain cash balances at financial institutions, which may at times exceed&#13;the amounts insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation. Management does not believe there is significant credit risk&#13;associated with these financial institutions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Sales to Wal-Mart&amp;#174;&#13;comprised 35.7% of revenues in fiscal year 2019 and 31.9% of total accounts receivable was due from Wal-Mart&amp;#174; as of November&#13;1, 2019. Sales to Wal-Mart&amp;#174; comprised 36.4% of revenues in fiscal year 2018 and 31.3% of total accounts receivable was due&#13;from Wal-Mart&amp;#174; as of November 2, 2018. Sales to Dollar General&amp;#174; comprised 11.1% of revenues in fiscal year 2019 and 21.7%&#13;of total accounts receivable was due from Dollar General&amp;#174; as of November 1, 2019. Sales to Dollar General&amp;#174; comprised&#13;9.6% of revenues in fiscal year 2018 and 23.5% of total accounts receivable was due from Dollar General&amp;#174; as of November 2,&#13;2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 7.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Business segments&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our company and subsidiaries&#13;operate in two business segments - the processing and distribution of frozen foods products, and the processing and distribution&#13;of snack food products. See Note 7 for further information.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fiscal year&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We maintain our accounting&#13;records on a 52-53-week fiscal basis ending on the Friday closest to October 31. As part of the regular accounting cycle, fiscal&amp;#160;years&amp;#160;2019&#13;and 2018 included 52 weeks.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenues&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The Company recognizes revenue&#13;for the sale of the product at the point in time when our performance obligation has been satisfied and control of the product&#13;has transferred to our customer, which generally occurs upon shipment, pickup or delivery to a customer based on terms of the sale.&#13;Contracts with customers are typically short-term in nature with completion of a single performance obligation. Product is sold&#13;to foodservice, retail, institutional and other distribution channels. Products are delivered to customers primarily through our&#13;own long-haul fleet, common carrier or through a Company owned direct store delivery system. These delivery costs, $5,012 and $3,883&#13;for fiscal years 2019 and 2018, respectively, are included in selling, general and administrative expenses in the accompanying&#13;consolidated financial statements. Shipping and handling that occurs after the customer has obtained control of the product is&#13;recorded as a fulfillment cost rather than an additional assured service. Costs paid to third party brokers to obtain contracts&#13;are recognized as part of selling expenses. Other sundry items in context of the contract are also recognized as selling expense.&#13;Any taxes collected on behalf of the government are excluded from net revenue.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We record revenue at transaction&#13;price which is measured as the amount of consideration we anticipate to receive in exchange for providing product to our customers.&#13;Revenue is recognized as the net amount estimated to be received after deducting estimated or known amounts including variable&#13;consideration for discounts, trade allowances, consumer incentives, coupons, volume-based incentives, cooperative advertising,&#13;product returns and other such programs. Promotional allowances, including customer incentive and trade promotion activities, are&#13;recorded as a reduction to sales based on amounts estimated being due to customers, based primarily on historical utilization and&#13;redemption rates. Estimates are reviewed regularly until incentives or product returns are realized and the result of any such&#13;adjustments are known. Promotional allowances deducted from sales for fiscal years 2019 and 2018 were $11,105 and $8,840, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advertising expenses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Advertising and other&#13;promotional expenses are recorded as selling, general and administrative expenses. Advertising expenses for fiscal years 2019 and&#13;2018 were $2,574 and $2,713, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and cash equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We consider all investments&#13;with original maturities of three months or less to be cash equivalents. Cash equivalents include money market funds and treasury&#13;bills. Cash equivalents totaled $3,478 as of November 1, 2019 and $8,179 as of November 2, 2018. All material cash and cash equivalents&#13;as of November 1, 2019 were held at Wells Fargo Bank N.A.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair value measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We classify levels of inputs to measure the&#13;fair value of financial assets as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 11pt Calibri
 Helvetica
 Sans-Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Level 1 inputs: Level 1 inputs are quoted market prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that are accessible at the measurement date.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Level 2 inputs: Level 2 inputs are from other than quoted market prices included in Level 1 that are observable for the asset or liability, either directly or indirectly.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Level 3 inputs: Level 3 inputs are unobservable and should be used to measure fair value to the extent that observable inputs are not available.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The hierarchy noted above&#13;requires us to minimize the use of unobservable inputs and to use observable market data, if available, when determining fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The Company does not have&#13;any assets or liabilities measured at fair value on a recurring or non-recurring basis for the fiscal years ended November 1, 2019&#13;and November 2, 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Inventories are valued&#13;at the lower of cost (which approximates actual cost on a first-in, first-out basis) or net realizable value. Inventories include&#13;the cost of raw materials, labor and manufacturing overhead. We regularly review inventory quantities on hand and write down any&#13;excess or obsolete inventories to net realizable value. An inventory reserve is created when potentially slow-moving or obsolete&#13;inventories are identified in order to reflect the appropriate inventory value. Changes in economic conditions, production requirements,&#13;and lower than expected customer demand could result in additional obsolete or slow-moving inventory that cannot be sold or must&#13;be sold at reduced prices and could result in additional reserve provisions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property, plant and equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Property, plant and equipment&#13;are carried at cost less accumulated depreciation. Major renewals and improvements are charged to the asset accounts while the&#13;cost of maintenance and repairs is charged to expense as incurred. When assets are sold or otherwise disposed of, the cost and&#13;accumulated depreciation are removed from the respective accounts and the resulting gain or loss is credited or charged to income.&#13;Depreciation is computed on a straight-line basis over 10 to 20 years for buildings and improvements, 5 to 10 years for machinery&#13;and equipment, and 3 to 5 years for transportation equipment. We are building a processing plant from the ground up and as such&#13;have attributed&amp;#160;long&amp;#160;useful lives&amp;#160;accordingly&amp;#160;to these types of assets employed at the new facility in Chicago.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Leases&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Leased property and equipment&#13;that meet lease criteria are capitalized at the lower of the present value of the minimum payments required under the lease or&#13;the fair value of the asset at inception of the lease and are included within property, plant and equipment on the consolidated&#13;balance sheet. If any, obligations under capital leases are accounted for as current and noncurrent liabilities on the consolidated&#13;balance sheet. Amortization is calculated on a straight-line method based upon the shorter of the estimated useful life of the&#13;asset or the lease term.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Life insurance policies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We record the cash surrender&#13;value or contract value for life insurance policies as an adjustment of premiums paid in determining the expense or income to be&#13;recognized under the contract for the period. The cash surrender value is included in other non-current assets in the accompanying&#13;consolidated balance sheets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Deferred taxes are provided&#13;for items whose financial and tax bases differ. A valuation allowance is provided against deferred tax assets when it is expected&#13;that it is more likely than not that the related asset will not be fully realized. The determination as to whether or not a deferred&#13;tax asset can be fully realized is subject to a significant degree of judgment, based at least partially upon a projection of future&#13;taxable income, which takes into consideration past and future trends in profitability, customer demand, supply costs, and multiple&#13;other factors, which are inherently difficult to predict.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We provide tax accruals&#13;for federal, state and local exposures relating to audit results, tax planning initiatives and compliance responsibilities. The&#13;development of these accruals requires judgments about tax issues, potential outcomes and timing. (See Note 4 to the Consolidated&#13;Financial Statements). Although the outcome of these tax audits is uncertain, in management&amp;#8217;s opinion adequate provisions&#13;for income taxes have been made for potential liabilities emanating from these reviews. If actual outcomes differ materially from&#13;these estimates, they could have a material impact on our results of operations.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-based compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We measure and recognize&#13;compensation expense for all share-based payments to employees, including grants of employee stock options, in the financial statements&#13;based on the fair value at the date of the grant. We have not issued, awarded, granted or entered into any stock-based payment&#13;agreements since April 29,&amp;#160;1999, and no such expense was recognized in fiscal years 2019 and 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Comprehensive income or loss&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Comprehensive income or loss consists of net&#13;income and additional minimum pension liability adjustments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recently issued accounting&#13;pronouncements and regulations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In May 2014, the Financial&#13;Accounting Standards Board (the &amp;#8220;FASB&amp;#8221;) issued ASU 2014-09 &amp;#8220;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&amp;#8221; to supersede&#13;previous revenue recognition guidance under current U.S. GAAP. The guidance presents a single five-step model for comprehensive&#13;revenue recognition that requires an entity to recognize revenue to depict the transfer of promised goods or services to customers&#13;in an amount that reflects the consideration to which the entity expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.&#13;Two options are available for implementation of the standard which are either the retrospective approach or cumulative effect adjustment&#13;approach. The guidance become effective for annual reporting periods that begin after December 15, 2017, including interim periods&#13;within that reporting period, with early adoption permitted. The Company adopted the modified retrospective transition method beginning&#13;with the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The adoption did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements. For&#13;further information please refer to Part I, Item 1, Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements under Revenues. Disaggregated revenue&#13;is disclosed in Part I, Item 1, Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements, Note 7: Segment Information.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In January 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-01, &amp;#8220;Recognition and Measurement of Financial Assets and Financial Liabilities&amp;#8221; that requires most&#13;equity investments to be measured at fair value and subsequent changes in fair value to be recognized in net income. The guidance&#13;covers presentation and disclosure requirements of financial liabilities and the classification and measurement of financial instruments.&#13;The guidance is effective for annual reporting periods and interim periods within those annual reporting periods beginning after&#13;December 15, 2017. We adopted this guidance in the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The adoption did not have a material impact on&#13;our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2016, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2016-02, &amp;#8220;Leases&amp;#8221;, which requires a lessee to recognize assets and liabilities with lease terms of&#13;more than 12 months. Both capital and operating leases are to be recognized on the balance sheet. The guidance is effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 and interim periods within fiscal years beginning after December 15,&#13;2019 which is our first quarter of fiscal 2020. We have analyzed all lease transactions during fiscal year 2019. The Company elected&#13;not to reassess expired contracts or adjust comparative periods. The Company determined that no change to current accounting treatment&#13;is warranted due to the underlying nature of our leases. In the case of month-to-month lease or rental agreements with terms of&#13;12 months or less, the Company made an accounting policy election to not recognize lease assets and liabilities. The Company performed&#13;a detailed analysis and determined that there were no indicators of longer-term leases at this time. The application of this pronouncement&#13;will result in additional disclosures detailing our lease arrangements. The Company continues to evaluate this statement and its&#13;impact on its results of operations or financial position but do not expect a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In October 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-16, &amp;#8220;Income Taxes &amp;#8211; Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments&amp;#8221;. The guidance&#13;involves eight specific cash flow issues and aims to unify accounting for these transactions. The guidance becomes effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early adoption permitted. The Company adopted this guidance during&#13;the first quarter of fiscal 2019 and it did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In March 2017, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2017-07, &amp;#8220;Compensation &amp;#8211; Retirement Benefits&amp;#8221;. The guidance separates service cost from other pension&#13;cost components changing the presentation of net periodic benefit cost related to company sponsored defined benefit or other postretirement&#13;benefits. The guidance becomes effective for annual and interim reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early&#13;adoption permitted. Additional disclosure reconciling net periodic benefit cost is detailed in Item I, Notes to the Consolidated&#13;Financial Statements under Note 3, Retirement and Other Benefit Plans. The Company adopted this guidance during the first quarter&#13;of fiscal 2019 and it did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2018, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2018-02, &amp;#8220;Income Statement-Reporting Comprehensive Income (Topic 220): Reclassification of Certain Tax Effects&#13;from Accumulated Other Comprehensive Income&amp;#8221;. The guidance allows reclassification from accumulated other comprehensive income&#13;to retained earnings for stranded tax effects resulting from the application of the U.S. Tax Cuts and Jobs Act. The guidance is&#13;effective for annual and interim reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 with early adoption permitted. The Company&#13;elected to early adopt this guidance during the quarter ended January 26, 2018. Adoption of this guidance had a material impact&#13;on retained earnings and other comprehensive income (see the Consolidated Statements of Shareholders&amp;#8217; Equity contained in&#13;this Report).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 6-&amp;#160;&lt;i&gt;Contingencies and Commitments:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 30pt&gt;The Company leases warehouse&#13;and/or office facilities throughout the United States and Canada through month-to-month rental agreements. In the case of month-to-month&#13;lease or rental agreements with terms of 12 months or less, the Company made an accounting policy election to not recognize lease&#13;assets and liabilities due to their underlying nature.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 30pt&gt;The Company leases three&#13;long-haul trucks received during fiscal 2019. Six-year leases for semi-trucks expire in 2025. Amortization of equipment under capital&#13;lease was $34 in 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 30pt&gt;The following is a schedule&#13;by years of future minimum lease payments for transportation leases:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 7 -&amp;#160;&lt;i&gt;Segment Information:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We have two reportable operating&#13;segments, Frozen Food Products (the processing and distribution of frozen products) and Snack Food Products (the processing and&#13;distribution of meat and other convenience foods).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We evaluate each segment&amp;#8217;s&#13;performance based on revenues and operating income. Selling, general and administrative expenses include corporate accounting,&#13;information systems, human resource and marketing management at the corporate level. These activities are allocated to each operating&#13;segment based on revenues and/or actual usage.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;(2,274&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Valuation allowance established against state NOL&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; padding-left: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Deferred income tax assets, net&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;4,047&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;4,010&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Management is required to evaluate whether&#13;a valuation allowance should be established against its deferred tax assets based on the consideration of all available evidence&#13;using a &amp;#34;more likely than not&amp;#34; standard. Realization of deferred tax assets is dependent upon taxable income in prior carryback&#13;years, estimates of future taxable income, tax planning strategies, and reversals of existing taxable temporary differences.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;As of November 1, 2019, the Company did not&#13;have any valuation allowance against its federal net deferred tax assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Management reevaluated the need for a valuation&#13;allowance at the end of 2019 and determined that some of its California NOL may not be utilized. Therefore, a valuation allowance&#13;of $77 has been retained for such portion of California NOL.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;As of November 1, 2019, the Company had net&#13;operating loss carryforwards of approximately $9,979 for federal and $874 for state purposes. The federal loss will be carried&#13;forward indefinitely until it can be utilized against future taxable income. The state loss carryforwards will expire at various&#13;dates from 2023 through 2034.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;As of November 1, 2019, we have provided a&#13;liability of $90 for unrecognized tax benefits related to various federal and state income tax matters. None of this liability&#13;will reduce our effective income tax rate if the asset is recognized in future reporting periods. We have not identified any new&#13;unrecognized tax benefits.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;As of November 2, 2018, we have provided a&#13;liability of $155 for unrecognized tax benefits related to various federal and state income tax matters. None of this liability&#13;will reduce our effective income tax rate if the asset is recognized in future reporting periods. We have not identified any new&#13;unrecognized tax benefits.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;We recognize any future accrued interest and&#13;penalties related to unrecognized tax benefits in income tax expense. As of November 1, 2019, we had approximately $18 in accrued&#13;interest and penalties which is included as a component of the $90 unrecognized tax benefit noted above.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Our federal income tax returns are open to&#13;audit under the statute of limitations for the fiscal years 2016 through 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;We are subject to income tax in California&#13;and various other state taxing jurisdictions. Our state income tax returns are open to audit under the statute of limitations for&#13;the fiscal years ended 2015 through 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;We do not anticipate a significant change to&#13;the total amount of unrecognized tax benefits within the next 12 months.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On December 22, 2017, President Trump signed&#13;into law the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act (the &amp;#8220;Tax Act&amp;#8221;). The Tax Act includes significant changes to the U.S. tax code that&#13;affected our fiscal year ended November 2, 2018, and future periods, including, but not limited to, (1) reduced the corporate federal&#13;income tax rate from 35% to 21%, (2) bonus depreciation that allowed for full expensing of qualified property in the year placed&#13;in service, and (3) the repeal of the domestic production activity deduction beginning with our fiscal year 2019. Section 15 of&#13;the Internal Revenue Code (the &amp;#8220;Code&amp;#8221;) stipulates that our fiscal year ended November 2, 2018 had a blended corporate&#13;tax rate of 23.07%, which is based on the applicable tax rates before and after the Tax Act and the number of days in the year.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Under U.S. GAAP, specifically ASC Topic 740,&#13;&lt;i&gt;Income Taxes,&lt;/i&gt; the tax effects of changes in tax laws must be recognized in the period in which the law is enacted, or December&#13;22, 2017, for the Tax Act. ASC Topic 740 also requires deferred tax assets and liabilities to be measured at the enacted tax rate&#13;expected to apply when temporary differences are to be realized or settled. Thus, at the date of enactment, the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;deferred taxes were re-measured based upon the new tax rates.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 3 -&amp;#160;&lt;i&gt;Retirement and Other Benefit Plans:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Noncontributory-Trusteed&#13;Defined Benefit Retirement Plans for Sales, Administrative, Supervisory and Certain Other Employees&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We have noncontributory-trusteed&#13;defined benefit retirement plans for sales, administrative, supervisory and certain other employees. In the third quarter of fiscal&#13;year 2006, we froze future benefit accruals under these plans for employees classified within the administrative, sales or supervisory&#13;job classifications or within any non-bargaining class. The benefits under these plans are primarily based on years of service&#13;and compensation levels. The funding policy of the plans requires contributions which are at least equal to the minimum required&#13;contributions needed to avoid a funding deficiency. The measurement date for the plans is our fiscal year end.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;8,768&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We perform an internal&#13;rate of return analysis when making the discount rate selection. The discount rates were based on FTSE Pension Liability Index&#13;(formerly Citibank) as of October 31, 2019 and September 30, 2018, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Plan assets are primarily&#13;invested in marketable equity securities, corporate and government debt securities and are administered by an investment management&#13;company. The plans&amp;#8217; long-term return on assets is based on the weighted-average of the plans&amp;#8217; investment allocation&#13;as of the measurement date and the published historical returns for those types of asset categories, taking into consideration&#13;inflation rate forecasts. Our expected employer contribution to the plans in fiscal year 2020 is zero.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;For fiscal year 2019,&#13;our actuary updated mortality tables from the mortality projection scale using MP-2017 Scaling to MP-2018 Scaling. The expected&#13;rate of return on plan assets remained the same at 7.00% effective for fiscal years 2019 and 2018, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Executive Retirement Plans&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Non-Qualified Deferred Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Effective January 1, 1991,&#13;we adopted a deferred compensation savings plan for certain key employees. Under this arrangement, selected employees contribute&#13;a portion of their annual compensation to the plan. We contribute an amount to each participant&amp;#8217;s account by computing an&#13;investment return equal to Moody&amp;#8217;s Average Seasoned Bond Rate plus 2%. Employees receive vested amounts upon death, termination&#13;or attainment of retirement age. No benefit expense was recorded under this plan for fiscal years 2019 and 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Supplemental Executive Retirement Plan&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In fiscal year 1991, we&#13;adopted a non-qualified supplemental retirement plan for certain key employees. Benefits provided under the plan are equal to 60%&#13;of the employee&amp;#8217;s final average earnings, less amounts provided by our defined benefit pension plan and amounts available&#13;through Social Security.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Benefits payable related&#13;to these plans and included in the accompanying consolidated financial statements were&amp;#160;$6,428&amp;#160;and&amp;#160;$5,553&amp;#160;as&#13;of November 1, 2019 and November 2, 2018, respectively. In connection with these arrangements we are the beneficiary of life insurance&#13;policies on the lives of certain key employees and retirees. The aggregate cash surrender value of these policies, included in&#13;non-current assets, was&amp;#160;$12,289&amp;#160;and $11,624 as of November 1, 2019 and November 2, 2018, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Incentive Compensation Plan for Certain Key Executives&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We provide an incentive&#13;compensation plan for certain key executives, which is based upon our pretax income. The payment of these amounts is generally&#13;deferred over three or five-year periods. The total amount payable related to this arrangement was $7,919 and $9,283 as of November&#13;1, 2019 and November 2, 2018, respectively. Future payments are approximately $4,264, $2,283, $1,221, $101 and $50 for fiscal years&#13;2020 through 2024, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Postretirement Healthcare Benefits for Selected Executive Employees&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We provide postretirement&#13;health care benefits for selected executive employees. Net periodic postretirement healthcare (benefit) cost is determined using&#13;assumptions as of the beginning of each fiscal year, except for the total actual benefit payments and the discount rate used to&#13;develop the net periodic postretirement benefit expense, which is determined at the end of the fiscal year.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 5 -&amp;#160;&lt;i&gt;Line of Credit and Borrowing&#13;Agreement:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;We maintain a line of credit with Wells Fargo&#13;Bank, N.A. that expires on March 1, 2020. Under the terms of this line of credit, we may borrow up to $7,500 at an interest rate&#13;equal to the bank&amp;#8217;s prime rate or LIBOR plus 1.5%. The borrowing agreement contains various covenants, the more significant&#13;of which require us to maintain a minimum tangible net worth, a minimum quick ratio, a minimum net income after tax and total capital&#13;expenditures less than&amp;#160;$7,500. The Company was in violation of the capital expenditure covenant&amp;#160;at November 1, 2019&amp;#160;which&#13;was subsequently waived (per letter dated&amp;#160;December 16,&amp;#160;2019). The Company borrowed $2,000 under this line of credit on&#13;April 15, 2019, which was repaid on April 25, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On December 26, 2018, we entered into a master&#13;collateral loan and security agreement with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A for up to $15,000 in equipment financing. Pursuant to the loan&#13;agreement, we&amp;#160;made two borrowings&amp;#160;of $7,500 each, to purchase specific equipment for our new Chicago processing facility&#13;at a fixed rate of 4.13% and 3.98%, respectively, per annum. The loan terms are seven years and are secured by the purchased equipment.&#13;The first funding of $7,500 was received on December 28, 2018. The second funding was received on April 23, 2019. The master collateral&#13;loan and security agreement with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. contains various affirmative and negative covenants that limit the use&#13;of funds and define other provisions of the loan. The main financial covenants are listed below:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 11pt Calibri
 Helvetica

 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Total Liabilities divided by Tangible Net Worth&amp;#160;(as defined)&amp;#160;not greater than 2.5 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter,&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Quick Ratio&amp;#160;(as defined)&amp;#160;not less than 1.0 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter end, and&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif&gt;Net income after taxes not less than one dollar on a quarterly basis, determined as of each fiscal quarter end.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The first secured equipment note payable is&#13;due with monthly principal and interest payments of $103 commencing on January 31, 2019 for 84 monthly installments including interest&#13;of 4.13% per annum. The second secured equipment note payable is due with monthly principal and interest payments of $102 commencing&#13;on May 31, 2019 for 84 monthly installments including interest of 3.98% per annum.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

The master collateral loan and security agreement with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. contains various&#13;affirmative and negative covenants that limit the use of funds and define other provisions of the loan.
