 Serif&gt;Total Liabilities divided by Tangible Net Worth not greater than 2.5 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter,&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Quick Ratio not less than 1.0 to 1.0 at each fiscal quarter end,&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Net income after taxes not less than one dollar on a quarterly basis, determined as of each fiscal quarter end.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The Company maintains a&#13;line of credit with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. that expires on March 1, 2020. Under the terms of this line of credit, we may borrow&#13;up to $7,500 at an interest rate equal to the bank&amp;#8217;s prime rate or LIBOR plus 1.5%. The Company borrowed $2,000 under this&#13;line of credit on November 24, 2019. The Company borrowed an additional 2.500,000 under the line of credit on January 23, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of estimates and assumptions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The preparation of financial&#13;statements in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make certain estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities at the date of the&#13;financial statements, as well as the reported revenues and expenses during the respective reporting periods. Actual results could&#13;differ from those estimates. Amounts estimated related to liabilities for pension benefits, self-insured workers&amp;#8217; compensation&#13;and employee healthcare benefits are subject to inherent uncertainties and these estimated liabilities may ultimately settle at&#13;amounts which may vary from current estimates. Other areas with underlying estimates include realization of deferred tax assets,&#13;cash surrender or contract value of life insurance policies, promotional allowances and the allowance for doubtful accounts and&#13;inventory reserves. Management believes its current estimates are reasonable and based on the best information available at the&#13;time.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations of credit risk&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our credit risk is diversified&#13;across a broad range of customers and geographic regions. Losses due to credit risk have recently been immaterial. The carrying&#13;amount of cash equivalents, accounts and other receivables, accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximate fair market value&#13;due to the short maturity of these instruments. We maintain cash balances at financial institutions, which may at times exceed&#13;the amounts insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation. Management does not believe there is significant credit risk&#13;associated with these financial institutions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Business segments&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fiscal year&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenues&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The Company recognizes revenue&#13;for the sale of the product at the point in time when our performance obligation has been satisfied and control of the product&#13;has transferred to our customer, which generally occurs upon shipment, pickup or delivery to a customer based on terms of the sale.&#13;Contracts with customers are typically short-term in nature with completion of a single performance obligation. Product is sold&#13;to foodservice, retail, institutional and other distribution channels. Products are delivered to customers primarily through our&#13;own long-haul fleet, common carrier or through a Company owned direct store delivery system. These delivery costs, $5,012 and $3,883&#13;for fiscal years 2019 and 2018, respectively, are included in selling, general and administrative expenses in the accompanying&#13;consolidated financial statements. Shipping and handling that occurs after the customer has obtained control of the product is&#13;recorded as a fulfillment cost rather than an additional assured service. Costs paid to third party brokers to obtain contracts&#13;are recognized as part of selling expenses. Other sundry items in context of the contract are also recognized as selling expense.&#13;Any taxes collected on behalf of the government are excluded from net revenue.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advertising expenses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and cash equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair value measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We classify levels of inputs to measure the&#13;fair value of financial assets as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 1 inputs: Level 1 inputs are quoted market prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that are accessible at the measurement date. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 2 inputs: Level 2 inputs are from other than quoted market prices included in Level 1 that are observable for the asset or liability, either directly or indirectly.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 3 inputs: Level 3 inputs are unobservable and should be used to measure fair value to the extent that observable inputs are not available.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The hierarchy noted above&#13;requires us to minimize the use of unobservable inputs and to use observable market data, if available, when determining fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property, plant and equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Life insurance policies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Deferred taxes are provided&#13;for items whose financial and tax bases differ. A valuation allowance is provided against deferred tax assets when it is expected&#13;that it is more likely than not that the related asset will not be fully realized. The determination as to whether or not a deferred&#13;tax asset can be fully realized is subject to a significant degree of judgment, based at least partially upon a projection of future&#13;taxable income, which takes into consideration past and future trends in profitability, customer demand, supply costs, and multiple&#13;other factors, which are inherently difficult to predict.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-based compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Comprehensive income or loss&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recently issued accounting&#13;pronouncements and regulations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In May 2014, the Financial&#13;Accounting Standards Board (the &amp;#8220;FASB&amp;#8221;) issued ASU 2014-09 &amp;#8220;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&amp;#8221; to supersede&#13;previous revenue recognition guidance under current U.S. GAAP. The guidance presents a single five-step model for comprehensive&#13;revenue recognition that requires an entity to recognize revenue to depict the transfer of promised goods or services to customers&#13;in an amount that reflects the consideration to which the entity expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.&#13;Two options are available for implementation of the standard which are either the retrospective approach or cumulative effect adjustment&#13;approach. The guidance become effective for annual reporting periods that begin after December 15, 2017, including interim periods&#13;within that reporting period, with early adoption permitted. The Company adopted the modified retrospective transition method beginning&#13;with the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The adoption did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements. For&#13;further information please refer to Part I, Item 1, Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements under Revenues. Disaggregated revenue&#13;is disclosed in Part I, Item 1, Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements, Note 7: Segment Information.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In January 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-01, &amp;#8220;Recognition and Measurement of Financial Assets and Financial Liabilities&amp;#8221; that requires most&#13;equity investments to be measured at fair value and subsequent changes in fair value to be recognized in net income. The guidance&#13;covers presentation and disclosure requirements of financial liabilities and the classification and measurement of financial instruments.&#13;The guidance is effective for annual reporting periods and interim periods within those annual reporting periods beginning after&#13;December 15, 2017. We adopted this guidance in the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The adoption did not have a material impact on&#13;our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2016, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2016-02, &amp;#8220;Leases&amp;#8221;, which requires a lessee to recognize assets and liabilities with lease terms of&#13;more than 12 months. Both capital and operating leases are to be recognized on the balance sheet. The guidance is effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 and interim periods within fiscal years beginning after December 15,&#13;2019 which is our first quarter of fiscal 2020. We have analyzed all lease transactions during fiscal year 2019. The Company elected&#13;not to reassess expired contracts or adjust comparative periods. The Company determined that no change to current accounting treatment&#13;is warranted due to the underlying nature of our leases. In the case of month-to-month lease or rental agreements with terms of&#13;12 months or less, the Company made an accounting policy election to not recognize lease assets and liabilities. The Company performed&#13;a detailed analysis and determined that there were no indicators of longer-term leases at this time. The application of this pronouncement&#13;will result in additional disclosures detailing our lease arrangements. The Company continues to evaluate this statement and its&#13;impact on its results of operations or financial position but do not expect a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In October 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-16, &amp;#8220;Income Taxes &amp;#8211; Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments&amp;#8221;. The guidance&#13;involves eight specific cash flow issues and aims to unify accounting for these transactions. The guidance becomes effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early adoption permitted. The Company adopted this guidance during&#13;the first quarter of fiscal 2019 and it did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In March 2017, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2017-07, &amp;#8220;Compensation &amp;#8211; Retirement Benefits&amp;#8221;. The guidance separates service cost from other pension&#13;cost components changing the presentation of net periodic benefit cost related to company sponsored defined benefit or other postretirement&#13;benefits. The guidance becomes effective for annual and interim reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early&#13;adoption permitted. Additional disclosure reconciling net periodic benefit cost is detailed in Item I, Notes to the Consolidated&#13;Financial Statements under Note 3, Retirement and Other Benefit Plans. The Company adopted this guidance during the first quarter&#13;of fiscal 2019 and it did not have a material impact on our consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2018, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2018-02, &amp;#8220;Income Statement-Reporting Comprehensive Income (Topic 220): Reclassification of Certain Tax Effects&#13;from Accumulated Other Comprehensive Income&amp;#8221;. The guidance allows reclassification from accumulated other comprehensive income&#13;to retained earnings for stranded tax effects resulting from the application of the U.S. Tax Cuts and Jobs Act. The guidance is&#13;effective for annual and interim reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 with early adoption permitted. The Company&#13;elected to early adopt this guidance during the quarter ended January 26, 2018. Adoption of this guidance had a material impact&#13;on retained earnings and other comprehensive income (see the Consolidated Statements of Shareholders&amp;#8217; Equity contained in&#13;this Report).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Net pension cost consisted of the following:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Weighted average assumptions for each fiscal&#13;year are as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
